A dedicated Android application that turns your device into a lightweight “ROM‑hacker” and management tool for classic console game ROMs. It is designed for people who want to edit, organize, or tweak ROM files directly on a phone or tablet.

| What it does | How it helps |
|--------------|--------------|
| **Browse and manage ROM libraries** | View your ROM collection in a clean, sortable list. Search, filter, and group by platform (NES, SNES, GBA, etc.). |
| **Edit metadata** | Rename files, add comments, tags, or custom attributes, and keep your collection clean and searchable. |
| **Open and edit ROM contents** | With the built‑in viewer, you can open a ROM and explore its internal file structure (images, sound, code). |
| **Replace assets** | Drop a new image or audio file onto a ROM entry to replace the original file—no need to unpack, edit, and repack manually. |
| **Hex editing** | For advanced users, a small hex editor lets you tweak raw bytes inside the ROM. |
| **Backup & restore** | Quickly back up ROMs to external storage or cloud, and restore them if something goes wrong. |
| **Export to PC** | Sync edited ROMs to a computer for further work or to upload to an emulator. |
| **Auto‑detect emulators** | Detects installed emulators on the device and can launch the ROM directly from ROM Toolbox. |
| **User‑friendly UI** | Designed for touch—tap to select, swipe to replace, long‑press for context actions. |

**Typical use‑cases**

1. **Quick fixes** – e.g., change a sprite or level map on the fly while playing on an emulator.
2. **Organizing a library** – tag ROMs with genres or languages, create playlists for a party night.
3. **Learning ROM hacking** – experiment with small edits without juggling a PC‑based toolkit.

Below is the full list of helper functions that *could* be used if the tool set were enabled (you’ll see the function name, what it does, and its main arguments).

| Function | Purpose | Key arguments |
|----------|---------|---------------|
| `bash_execute` | Run a shell command safely (with whitelist/timeout). | `command`, `timeout`, `working_directory` |
| `grep_search` | Regex‑based text search in files. | `pattern`, `path`, `glob_pattern`, `case_sensitive`, `context_lines` |
| `code_search` | Semantic search for symbols (functions, classes, methods). | `query`, `path`, `symbol_type`, `case_sensitive` |
| `find_references` | Find usages of a symbol across the codebase. | `symbol`, `path`, `scope`, `case_sensitive`, `include_definition` |
| `read_file` | Read a text file or a PDF page range. | `file_path`, `offset`, `limit`, `start_page`, `end_page` |
| `create_file` | Create a new file (optionally overwrite). | `file_path`, `content`, `overwrite`, `dry_run` |
| `edit_file_lines` | Edit specific line ranges in a file. | `file_path`, `line_edits`, `expected_hash`, `dry_run` |
| `edit_file_search_replace` | Search‑replace blocks with tolerance. | `file_path`, `edits`, `tolerance`, `expected_hash`, `dry_run` |
| `append_to_file` | Append text to the end of a file. | `file_path`, `content`, `create_if_missing`, `dry_run` |
| `delete_file` | Delete a file (always requires approval). | `file_path`, `dry_run` |
| `read_url` | Download and convert a web page to markdown. | `url`, `use_fallback` |
| `web_search` | Perform a web search via Jina/Searx/DuckDuckGo. | `query`, `max_results`, `region`, `safesearch`, `engines`, `categories` |
| `wikipedia_search` | Fetch Wikipedia article summaries. | `query`, `max_results`, `chars_per_result` |
